Spirit
Vessel
Details

Details

Appearance
A very slender individual, her physical build strongly suggests she is frail. Ava weighs no more than ninety pounds, but despite her still growing body and very childish features she still retains a familiar bit of feminine charm. The bare beginnings of an hourglass figure has started to change her build and is just a little visible, even under her usual layers of clothing. Her skin is incredibly pale, almost porcelain white, only adding to the overall sickly look she possesses. The Vessel's face is rounded and her cheeks still possess a healthy layer of baby fat, but the overall shape of her adorable features hold a striking resemblance to that of a certain regal Sorcerer's. That is about where their similarities in appearance end, however, since her big round awe-filled eyes are a bright purple rather than such an intense blue as his are, and the long baby-soft hair that trails down her back in a light veil is as white as snow.
(Height: 5'0" // Weight: 90 lbs. )

Attire
Her style is very distinct, and while the clothing she wears will certainly vary, every article she owns carries the same aesthetic formula. If Ava is wearing colors (as opposed to base black and white fabric) they are always varying shades of blue, red, and/or purple, she is never seen in anything else. Most commonly the aforementioned formula consists of a light blouse, a fluffy knee-length skirt that catches the air easily often leading to her wearing a pair of shorts underneath for the sake of modesty, heeled boots that stretch up her legs far enough to cover her ankles but not much more, a loose fitting open cloak style "jacket" that is often longer than her skirt and sags a little off her shoulders, and a wide brimmed floppy pointy hat. Charms and accessories--such as earrings, necklaces, etc--also vary far more vastly in style and shape than her base attire, but they still fall under the "red, blue, and purple only" rule.

Personality
Above all else, Ava is very curious. She expresses great interest in all new things, big or small, and is always willing to learn from new experiences and people alike. This is a defining quality of her overall demeanor, but not the only one. Equally noticeable is her strong will and overwhelming stubbornness, but even still there are other traits expertly hidden behind that obvious pair. She has quite the impressive amount of control over her own emotions despite being such a young girl, and while the telltale signs of her engaging actress mode are still apparent, they are incredibly hard to pinpoint or find without spending a lot of time getting to know her. She is manipulative, but not in the sense that causes others to be harmed or used, she just has a high capacity for controlling the elements of her own persona, and can use some of them to overshadow and hide others.

Details

She is manipulative, but not in the sense that causes others to be harmed or used, she just has a high capacity for controlling the elements of her own persona, and can use some of them to overshadow and hide others.

̷̨̠̪̤͈̼̤̝͉̬̫͖̰̱̱̓̿̉p̴̨̡̛̫̻͈͇̗͕̜̦͍̜̂͆̂͌̂͂̔̀̋͊̕͜͝͝͝ḽ̶̗̥̜̤͓͂̽̐̆̄̇̿̾̏͋̓̏̆a̴̢̭͉̮̣̘̭͙̻̪͊̍̏͂͛͜͠n̸̨̜͕͍̺̝͒̿̿͆̌̀̌̽͋̇͘e̶̢͓̱̼͍̝̼̻̬͋̈́͊̄̌͒̕s̴̡̡̭̜̥̲̤̺͍͚͓̜̪̦̍̎̃̌̈́͋͌̓̋͜ ̵̨̱̞̝͚̞̮̰͚̙̖̔̀̈́̎͛͐̑͝o̴̪͙̮͉͙̯̝̲̻͖̹͎̥̚ͅͅf̴̧̙̠̮̥̻̝͚͍̦̩̤̫̳͂͒̍̉̍͋͌͌ ̷̤͖̯̘̘͚͓͓̮̙̺̽̓̈̉͌͆̍͒̀̚͠͝ë̷̦̯͂x̵̢̢̙͇͕̰͕͙͍̜̟̫̜̖̄̅͑̄͜i̵̢̹̼̫̠̫͚̰͚͉͇̊̑̎̾̏̌̌̅̍͠s̸̢̤͉̮̝̮͇̠̓̄́̈́͝ͅt̶̨̧̨̰̹̦̮̜̼̘̟̹̭̾̀̈́̏e̵̟̙̣̖̟̜̣̫̟̦̺͈̗͌̒͐̉̈́̑̎̆͘͝͝n̵͓͔͕̹͊ͅc̷̼̖̠̣̠͈̙̭͔̦͓͚̹̼̈̃̈́̽̇͝͠e̶̛̠̲̺̺̼̙͈̳͖̖̐̐̃̈̀̎̈́͐́͠ ̷̬̻̞͎̦̼̄ͅk̸̢̘̯̂̍͌̆̈́͑̽̿̈́n̴͔̼̙̯̟̞̐̉̚ͅǫ̵̥̰̱͙͎̣̫͎̙̭͓̺̲̐͂̓̑̓w̸̝͚̩͉̹̘͚͔̝̫̦͝n̷̛͔̳̮̟̹͉̘̽̉̉̒̂͌̾͛͑̚̚ ̵͍͔̹̲̭͆̀̐ḁ̸͈͓̺̖͔͚̫̩̮̊̐̽͒͜͠s̷̛̯̫̺̥̫̬͚̈́̌̾̃͛͌͂̉̔̑̋͝ ̸͔͓̭̻͑̍̌͌̍̃͒̆̽͘͘“̸̛̲̦̼̝̜̰̙̺̉͗̆̿̽̀́͘͝T̶̖̜̙͚̎͋̊̈́͌̑̓͛̿͆͝h̷̛̺̺̫̠̉ẽ̷̤̟̲̖͌͒̋̐̿͑̿̄̄͜ ̴͓͍̪͐́̉̀̽̐̋̎̏̎͋͗B̶̻̝̦̍̑̋̅̾͌͒̃͠ḙ̴̛̫͕̇̂͛̍̏̓͐̀́̈́͠ͅt̸̛̛̜̰̬̳͚̺͇̟̤͕̓͊́̽̈̈́̅̈́̀̒w̴̧̪̓̿̂͊̒̊̂͋̈́̈̔͘̕͝͝e̸͈̙̠̘̭̺͚͙͕͔̎͛̏̾͌͌̓̋͋̂͝ḛ̵̡̗͚̺̫̘͎͎͕͚̤̂͒͋̍̋̓̇̕͘͝n̴̨̨͎͓̱̪̦̼̐̈͠͝.̸̢̣̥͚̫̮̝̦͎̺͎͕̋̐̑͆̂̅ͅ”̶̛̠̍̂̔̾̿ ̶͓̫̖͉͒Ş̷̲̜͍̥̮̘̊̓̉̄̔̇̊̎̀̒̍̕h̴̨̫̟̬̾́́͆̄ę̶͚̹̅̈́̆͂ ̶̡̡͙̰̼͓͙̣̪̾͂̏̒̔̊̋̅͂̀͒w̶̩͙͔̗͍̝̖͍͕͗̇̊̈͆́̓̐̄̐͘̚͜͝ă̵̠͚͎͈̈̚ͅs̶̠̬̺̊̂̍͋̀̌͋͗͒̊̉ ̶͇̭͙͖̰̟͙̭̓̅͌̒͂̈́̋̀̎́͘ć̵̢̮̗͆̉͊̐͒͗̇̀̏̀͝͝ä̶͉̣͇̲̦̣̞̿́̎̒͐͐̽̚͠͝ṟ̴̲̠͖͕͓͓̣̞̹̝͕̬͛̄̐͐͋̈́̿̔̂͐͒͝͝͝͝ͅȅ̵̼̩̫̗̺̱̠͈͈̈̏̽̍͑̂̑͗̈͘̕͠͝f̶̧̱̳̥̗̫̥͉̮͇̬̬̭͉͆̎́͜ṵ̴̅̂͊͐̓͑͂̾ḷ̸̳̞̹̤̹̤̱̎̽̓̈́̉̈̿́̆̍͛̀͝͝ḽ̴̤̮̝̥̻̫̭̬͇̣͒̈́̀͊͊͜ÿ̶̛̝̙̮̻̮͙̙̦͕̜͍̯̯́̀̆̉̑͂̓͋͗̿̑̚͠͝ ̶̨̧̦̜̠̭̳̻̙̪̖̻̝͚͂̊ͅg̸͉̉̌̄̆̔̐̓u̴̘̟̥͓͇̺̱͉͕̲̩̠̣̭͋̍͌̀̍̈̑̊͝ȧ̴̗̳̙̠̳̯̝͍̪͖̾̈̍̓͂̋̉̏̎̕ŗ̸͇̘̟̹̏d̶̢̛͙͔̯͍͓̜̖̣͉͍͍̪͋͆̑̐͒͂͗̄e̸̺̤͐͑̂̿̈̍̈́d̷̝̪̖̩͚͇͇̮̦̥̪̘̟̂͒̎͋͐̐̄̅̇̄̍̾͒̕͠ ̵̨͈͕̱̺̝̗͑͐͐̑̑̿̈́͋̍̃̇̈́͜͜͝b̷̨̨̺͕̩̫̬̱̖̳̻̭̅͒̅͑͊́́̀͘ͅý̸̨̡̢̡̤̹̜͎̲̜̞̱̦̲̈́͒̂̿͝ ̸͖̱̺͑̋̈́̆̈́͂͛͑̈́͊̍͛̃͝v̸̨͕͕͔̂͐͊̽̃͆͗̀͊͠ą̵̛̼̳̻͕̬̯͉͉͉͈̼̱͙̉͋͛̈́͂̅͊̓̇̈́͛̎͠͠r̵̨̢̯̻̣̰̤̝̙͐͊͆͠i̴̛̞̠͉͈̺̩̤͖͍͇͂̈́̈́͋̇͑͐̆̆̄̈͜͝o̷̤̭͓̠̖̥͔̼̙̪̹͈͕͓͒͆̃̈́ͅu̷̢̞͎̼̭̼̼̣̲̓̔̅ş̷̛͖̘̓̀͊̋̓̇͒̉̀̌ ̷̡̧̜̰̹̜̱̻̞͉̝̥̂̐̏̊̄̚͜͜ͅW̶̨̥̙͚̘̝̞̝̣̟͈͍̠̎̋́͋̐̓̌̎̎̽̌̏̌̕̕i̴̥͕͗̅̿̕l̷̢̨̳̺̤̫̠̠̙̻͖͇͑̒̄͋̍̾͗̑͒̊͒̉̔̓̐ͅl̷̨̧̟̲̪͙̼̳̦͔̙̃̉ͅ-̸̡̡̣̠̥͕͙͙̰̩̗̯͕̰̜̊̂̓͘͝ǒ̶̢̤͚̉̒̏̈́̆̄͝’̶̨̛̛̘͖͙͗̒̎̆͆͐̆͘-̵̼̜̭̀t̸̨̻͍̺͚̤͗̾͊̆̀͒͂̊́͝h̴̡̢̗͍̣̯̆͜é̴̛̠̠̻͇̰̤͖̩̖̬̥̀̽̈́̀͑͑̀͊̈́́̓͘-̷̗̎̆̑͌̈́̅̑̉̂̈͒̍͘W̴̪̖̣̘̳͇̲̭̜̽̿̇̽̏͐̋͌͌̌͝i̶̗̹̹͂̃̂͋̆̃͝s̷̙̘̭̓̀̈́̽͗͠͝ͅp̸̢̡̡̨̗͈̝̲̟͊̈̂̃͗̒ͅs̶̡̱̬̲̤̞̱̗̲̮̻͊-̷̛̠͍̥̜̣̲͖̦͔̗̠͑̃̋̋̽̓̈́͌̾̉͝-̸̢̨̨̼͙͈̜͓̝̝̻̻̍̓̏̾̆͛̆́͐͊̽̅̕͘̚͜ͅs̷̨̢̢̛̪͙̣̣̻̫̞̪̊̌̄́̓̀͊͊̽͒̓́̚p̶̱͈̻͌͌̓̍̆́̍͘͝e̸̜̣͕̪͓̟̥̬̋̀͐͝c̸͔̦̓͊͐͒̏̿͐̚̚̚͠͠͠i̷̢̦̙͓͍͇͎͍͇̬̤͈̻͐̄̃̈͜͠f̶̡̡̨̺̙̙̟̦͙̖̭̩͘i̵͚͖̭͗̉͑̇̏̌̈͒̓́͆c̴͍̲͉͎̺̼̻̻̃́̆͒̇̔̐͘͜ả̷͍̮̅̔̎̏͐͗̈̔̈́͒̓ĺ̸̛̬̬̰̮̮͎͚͓̆̇ͅļ̵̢̰̮̰̬̝̝̬̱̱́̔̊̌͑̓ͅͅẙ̵̢̬̼̝̱̳͓̩͖̝̪̞̝̳͚͒̋̽̇͒͆̅̑̈́̊͛ ̴̤͎͍̙́͝t̶̨̢̨̼̼͈̜̹̊̔̄̏̒̈́̎̈̂͋̑͝h̴̫̮̹͍͚͚͉͛͌̇̑͂̇̀͋́̃̏͆̈́ơ̸̢̧͕̼͓͖̿͒̆͂͗̉̈́̅̆̔̈́͛͘͘͜s̴̼͍̱̲̬͓͓͈̩̐̀̎̅͆̇̌͝e̵̼͙͕̫͚̼̘̼̦̙̰̟͚͋̑̽͒̃͝ͅ ̷̺̘̠̰̪̟̓̈́̇̍̈́̌̒̕͘ͅt̷̛͈͖̠́h̴̡̢̛͉̜̙̞̺̟̮͖̳̭͇͓̃͒̃̉͗̃̔̉̌̌̔̑̽̚͜a̷̛̛͕̰͑̔̔̀̌͝ţ̸̗͉̜̟͛͜ ̶̡̡̲̠͖̬̙̙͉͇̞͚̖͉̞̽͑̈́̃̽́̇̔r̸̛̝͎̝̻̙̩̱̅̀͛̎̀́̒́͘͝͝͝͠ȩ̷͈̣̻̬̫͙̏̀́̔̏̓͑͒͗͋̕͜͜͝ͅͅm̶̢̧̫̗̝̑͠ą̷̢̱̯͉̲̲͓̟̣͕̑̆̓͑͛̕̕͜͜͝i̵͕̍̇̇̈́̃͛́̄̐̍͐ń̶̛̹̺͙̪̻̱̱͇̾̃̌̋̑̈̌͒͘̚̚ͅę̶̩̥̬̺͕͉̼́d̴̨̨̨͎͖̠̠̗̻͕̗̞͉̍͜ ̵̢̙̮͕̹͇͓͔̮̈́L̵̡̰͇̯͈̪̩͒̌͋̂̓͝͠i̵̧̦̼͉̱̝̳̤̳̿̏̚g̵̨̡̓̇̇̀͋̄͊͒̔̀͊̉̆̕͝ͅh̴̡̲̫̬̯͙̟͖͎̐̽̐̉̍̆̆̑͛t̶̮͇͇͛̑̓̕ ̵̢̳̗̺̥̺̞͓̯̺̬̖̅̈́̾̊ͅơ̵̼̝͌̄͊͛̌́͆̎͂̀͝͝f̷̜͖̋̆̂̿̈́̽̈͗̈́͐̾̓̈́̕͜͝ ̸̢̭͙͖̣̱̞̭̙͖̙͑̇̄́͑́̌͆͌̾̉̏͝͠ͅH̸̡̨̡̻͙̞͈͇̲̰̝̯̺͎̃̐͗̽̽̀͂̓̀̕̚ͅȩ̴̫̟͚̳͎̖̤̔ą̸̞̱̲̹̳͙͔̞̟̙̇̉̔̃͌̊̏̋̓̾̆͊̂͝ͅr̴̢̻̟̫̮̜̠̃̈́̈̆͐͋̾͑͑̌̚ẗ̷̛̥̪̻̖̲́̓̈̐̆̌̐̚̚-̸͍̟͇͔̏͗͜-̴̡̛̟͓̦͕͕̤̥͈͎͕͇̀̒̽͋͒͗͂͘ͅw̷̢̰̟̫̬̜̗̙̭͛̀̿̔͋̌̂͛͑̈́́h̶̰̲̳̯̩̰̥̾́̿͒͒͒̉͆̀ͅi̶̳̝͙͖͈̫̳̦̤̖̞̫̠̒͒́͊̀̓̃̆͘l̸̢̡̢͙͙̮͚͈͍̲͍̿̿̿̏e̸̢͐͊͆̈́̊̓̌̎͆̇̓͗̊ ̴̧̨͇̲̝͇̤̭͔̝̩̌́͑́̇͐ş̷̳̺̯͉̝̞͓͔̍̿̊͒͒̈́͂͌͘͜͜͝ͅͅh̸̞͎͕͎̽̌̐̈́̅͊͂̐̈́̾̿̚e̷͙̠̣͕̞̼̮̹̞̤̰̓̌̈́͐͊̔̎͌̀̀͜͜͝͠ ̵̛̹̥̠͎͈͚̲̩̬̤̘̅́͒̽̊͑̑́̑̔p̷̮͓̳͎͌̓̑̏̔̈́̑̋̈́͆̔̌̚͝ư̴̛͚̳̟̲͚͍̝̦̠͙͔̟̞̙̺͒͑̋̃̇̒́̾̒͊̍͗͝ş̷̡̺͚͍͇̯̬͉̄̀̊̈̅͘̚͠͠ḩ̸̮̮̰͚͓̗̥͇̮̓͜ȩ̶̩̮̻͖̺̩̫̗̩͆͗͋̒̑͗͋́ͅḍ̷̢̢̹̲͚͚͔͇̹͍̳̠͉̾͗̏̿̑̚͠ ̷̢͔̗̭͔͈̙̝̥̱̗̼̪̞̄̽͗͠ͅh̷̠̆́͗͌̃̑̎̾̍̿̕̕ḙ̶͈͓͉̈́̒̆͒́̈́̾̇́̿̒̚̚r̸̢̨̠̙͍̜͇̦̱̬͚̺͉̹͆̆͑̓̄͝ ̶̺̯̼̞̩̜͔̳̗̳̪̼̔̓͜r̶͕̯̮͍͎̲̙̗̱̺͕͕̜̤͚͊͛̐̿̆̈́͛̎e̴̘̘̠͖͎̩̙̜̰̗̅͆̓̏̇̿͗̃͘ͅq̷̹̈́͆͆͌̽̍͐̔͆̕u̵̲̘͂͊ͅḛ̴̡̻̞̦̤̩̞̝̖͕̳͈̋̑͑͆̏̏̿̂̄̈́͆̓̅͘͝s̶̛̲͔̉̍̆̃͘ͅt̷̡̲̲̭͕̞̬̠̩͕̘̽̒̾̏ş̷̻̟͈̆̌ ̷̨̢̛̤͙̯̠̮͓͖̣̫̉͐̂͐͑̍͝͝w̵̨̡̧͉̞̮̹͇̝̺̥͎̪͖̋ę̷̛͕̫̬̞̠̺̠͉̼̤̥͍͓͑̍͊̊̔̇̀͒͜r̷͕͓̦͚͉͇̩̼̖̯̿͒̏̏̌̆ê̴̗̱͉̬̲͇͓͉͍͙̽͗̀́̓̓́̈͌̍̚͝ ̸̺̭̗̄̏͒͒̋͂͐͛̇̿̾̔͝͝͝s̴̡̢̧̠̰͉̦̬̯͔̜̰͎̤͐̒̇͠t̸̝̣̙͎̪̞͎͍̞̻̰̦͒̌̎ő̵̬̝͔̍̾͑͐͗̓̉̆̅͛̊͊̄̿ǹ̸̯̞̾ę̴̢̛̜̰͙̺̼͙̰͙͋͛͑̑͠ͅw̴̡̧̛̲͇͎̥̱̥̬̱͇̝̤̌̐̀̾́̈́̓̈́͒͒̃͜͜͝a̸̛͔̱̩͍̝̐͊́̍̋̇̏͊̑͂l̵̯͈͉̉͜ͅḷ̵̡̢̨̦̮̩͓̟̙̈̃͆ͅe̸̢̡͚͉̥̙̺͜͜͠d̴̦͚̞̼̤̼̟͖̠͓̈͝͝.̸̢̧̖̭̥͑̊̅̇̽͗̏̑͛͗ͅ

A̵̩̘͚̝̭̔̔̈́͒͊͋̍̒͋̓ ̷̢̣̜͑̓͋͋͗̆̽̎̍͌̽͠͠͠ŗ̵̡͓͍̼̗͈͖̜̣̥͋͜ͅè̷͖͙̩̟̘͇̲͚͓̪̫̗̃̄̉̈͋̈́̅̍̚̕͝f̵̢̹͇̝̜̞̞̜̲̱͉̣̝̼̓͂̽̿̄̽̏̂͗̅u̵̫̙̓͊̏͑͒s̵̡̨̩̾̋͛̚e̴̡͇̫͚͇͈̞͎̺̙̩̥̐̊̋̀̿͐̆͘͠d̸̨̨̡̛̛͔̞̰̭́̾̎̓ ̵̢͕̪̻̤̭̮̱̺̇̾̉̉́̈̓̊̏̕͝ẗ̸̢̧̧͓̰̤̮̱́͌͒͆͐͋͐̄̋̂͠ơ̴̢̛̻͉̰̮̦̦͓̲̘̤͇̱̩̒̅̐̎̽̏͋͝ ̵̢̨̞͚͈͈̖̭͠g̶̢̛̜̱̻̜̘͎̣̤͊̈̇̐͊́̉į̷̢̰̦̈́́̿͂́́̃̓̋̉͝v̵̢͉͖̙̹̼͌̈́͌̃̽̄̅̆̽̈́̔̇͜͝͝ë̵̪͕̰̟͉̖̣̖̹͇̠́ ̴͚͖́͜͜u̷͖͉̯̪͖͔̗̤̲͍͂̊̌̾̈̔̽̑̈́̇͘p̷͈̘̹͓̗͖̙̂̅ ̶̩̓̈́h̵̛̯̰̫̿̿̏̋͌̔͛̕͘o̴̞̠̻̺̺̙͖̮̳̽͆̾͜͜͝p̷̢̺̲̬̝͕̩͍̮̯͙̳̥̥̅͛̉̔̍͒̌̇ě̵͉́̓̑̕͝͝ ̸̟̙͂̀ą̷̢̡̣͉̻͉̳͇͍̤̮͉͔̟̑́̇̈́̔̓n̸̹̩̥͘d̷͇̹̺̪͎̓ ̷̨̧̛̬̟̝̯̜̻̮̳̟̾̈́̐̒̅̓͑̋̏ó̵̧̡̺̱͎̤̟͖̤͔̮̝̆͐̀͑̍͆͌ͅņ̵̼̤͚̩͕͛̇̀͗̿ȩ̸̛̗̱̞͙̭͑͒̋̒͋̾͛̓̐̾͐̕͜͠ ̴̛̺͕̮̤̠̻͗̐̅͑̓͂͂̄̔̓̓͘͝͠d̷̫̝͇̣͇̣̯̳̣͎͍͉̐͗̒̓̋ą̷̧͔̲̽̿̽̉̈́̈́̔̓̀y̶̢̗̻̦̗̖͌̏̈̏͝ ̸̞̝͎͈͇̻̿͆̽̍̇c̸̠̻͕̑̾̍͒̃͗̂͌̈́̐̚ȯ̴̧̫̞̘̲̫̻̣̫̙͚̗̼̪̟͂͛n̸̡̤̲͙̣͎̟̙̘̣̩͔̦̾̂̃͐̾͊̄͐̃̿͘͘v̶̮̖̥̎̍͒͋̃̇̓͐̔͘͠ĩ̴̡̪̘̤̝̞̗̅͛̆͗̔̇̋̂͐̔̂͌n̴̨̨̦͇̭̹̱̤͚̝̜͙̍̍̓̀̓͝c̷̥̯͕̪͕͓̖͎͖̺͓̹͗̌̎͘̕e̸͖͊ḑ̸̯̠̹͈͙̤̼͇̮̮̾̀̓͗̍͗̀ ̸̛̛͉̺̦̘̹̟̺̯̯̞͎̤̭͆͐̆͛̐̑̒͌̓͗̃ą̸̨͓̯̥͂̾̄̈́̓͋͌̍͘ ̶̢̖̳̲̗̣̣̞̜̦͓͎͑̀̈́̔͗̊͋̿̇̚͝f̴̡͚̣͚͉̼̳̯͎̥̰̀͂̂͆̓͋e̴̡̝̲̟͑̓͐͜w̸̤̰͚̯̞̽̽͌̎͒̿́̊̐̑ ̵̛̬͓̺͈̱̝͗̓̿̈́͑̕Ŵ̷͉͍̪̗͈͉́̆́̾͗́̅̔͗̋̕į̸̨̩̠͉͔̱̱͙̪͙͖̈́̂̿̈́͝s̶͓̼̉̎͂̋̎͌̔͋̓̀̂̀͌̚͝ṕ̴̲̦̦̱͋̒ş̵̗̜͚̪̠͐̊̎͂̀̎̒͒̈̕ ̷̮̳̲̫̖̲̭͈̣̖̖̮̘̩́t̵̢͓̻̫̜̻̣̩͓̮͆͜o̸̟̿̋̈͌̿̊̇̑̊̏̉͋̆̆̀ ̴̡̢͈̩̲̖̗̟̲̺̘̦̰̤̖̀̓̿̈́̔͊̀͠é̷̮̬̘̩̹̤̜͉̍̆̎̍ş̵̡̛̙̺̳̜̺͎̭͗̀̿̎̂̽͒̽̓̐̕c̷̮͙̤͔̝̺̼̲͔͙̘̄̈̌͑̎͋̿̉̕o̸͚͓̻̮̙̜̮̞̦͕̯̾̈́͛̔́̇̒͝r̸̨̛͍͍̻͐́̊́͘t̸̯̫̩̙̫͓̱͚̺̩̥̆̔̌͌͜ ̸̟̰̻̝̈́̓͠͝h̴̢̨͚̫̻̝̃̿̇̑̊è̷̝͉͍͔̳̪̬͕̂́̈́̑̿̎̆̓̚͝͝͠ř̷̢̡͖̰͈̀͑͊̾̄̃͒̋̈̚̚͝ ̴̱̠̘̺̰̽̈͑̀̎̋́͝ó̶̡̼̫̱͇̠̬͙̮̝̹̤͆̄ȗ̵̧̢̢̯̘̜̺͈̭̝͍̦̬̜́̈́̈́̾t̶̹̠͖͍̾̈́̅͑͘͝,̴̢̧̰̫̩̬̫̱͕͔̳̤͗̿̑́͋͗̀́̍ ̴̞̱̘͕̟̜͗̅̓̕ó̶͍̭̼̱͓̣̘̰̯͒̓̓̈́͊̄̆̿͛n̴͚̰̮̦̱̩̗̼͕̪̾͒̏́̉̊̈́̋̎̃͒̚͠l̴̘͖̅y̷̠̱̣̾͗͆̈̐̊̋̿̕ ̴̧̡̱̰̈̇̌̓͊̿̒̒͑͋̉̚͜t̶̛̩̫̻͙̰̻̗͕̖̥͙̮̼̠̀̽̃̽͂́͌́̄̆̈́͌͘͘ǫ̷̨̛̗̲͇̠͙͒̑͆̀͒͒́̿̂͘͘͝͝ ̴̰͉̺͚͕͎͉̮͈̓̄̾͝ͅͅf̸͍̗̮̜̟͆̈̈̃̋̀ì̷̼͕͈̙͈͓̅͗͛͊̄͐̿̚͜n̷̡̝͔͙̟̦̮͋̊̽̈́̌̿̽̇́d̵̡̙̱͈̟͉̭̪͑͝͠ ̷̨̧̛̩̳̲͉̯̻͍͖͔̱́͛̿̓̋͘͝ą̷̡̰͔̫͚̬͙̫̘̖̈́ ̶̪̖͎̬̪͎̥̺̙͗̊̏͐͋͂̔̀͜m̷̡͕̫̻̭̣̮̘̥͕͚̙̰͉͙̃̿̓̓͘̕͘a̶̙̱̰̫̦̤̳̿̂ͅĵ̴̝̦͂̀͠ȯ̸̢͇̗͖̪̱̲̼̯̠̰́̀̅̿̀͑́̍̈́́̚͠͝͝r̴͇͔̖̿͂̒̔͋̅̑ì̶̛̛̙̘̔͝t̶̝̲̠̋̊̃͗̚y̷͓͈̞̞͖̘͖̥͑̉̇̑̈́̍̓̽̈̀̍̔͘̚̚ ̷̢̥̖͚̪͇̟̻͚̑̒̂͜ͅȯ̷̗̺̮̬̤͙̑f̶̪̦͍̓̔̐͂̆́͗̿͊̀̇̾̓̆͜͠ ̴̧̛̪̭̘̞̦̲̭̘̙̲̣̞̂̒̈́́̏̅͆͒͘t̵͔̋̾̏́̄͆͘͠͠h̵̢̛̲͓̬͍̬̳͇̗̝̠̘̝͉͓̔̊̽͆́͆̓̚e̸̤͓̖̞̼̝͉͂̄̅̾̈́̌́̎̚̕͜ ̶̨̧̨̞̞̤̙͓̳͕̬̼̈́̈́̆̓͂͘͝ͅp̶̡̛̺̹͍͖̖̯̀̈͑̎̃̕͝ļ̵͔̱͔̦̦̦̬̼̲͖͔̉̂a̸̧̛͖̼̥̫̟̬̯̻̖̞͖͉̩͍̐̐̍n̷̛̩̬͓̥͙͖͇̬̈e̵̛͈̟͑͊̀́͜s̵͔͖̗̞̳̓̐̅̂ ̸͇̮̫̲̝̱͋͑̋̈i̷̢̧̛̺̣̞͓̯ṅ̴̡̻̱̟̟̳̮͖̲͉͔̫͓͐̔̿̿̈́̋̅ ̷̧̟̟̦͚̣̹͔̽̈͊̀̒͋̋͆̓́̓͌͊͜͜͠p̵̘̬̮̪̱̻̠͔͓̙̽̀̈́̆̆ͅe̸͍͇̝̠͇͍̦̺̮̞̳̟̾͑͊r̵̦̀̀̊̆̈́ị̸̡̨̱͉̖̜̟̎̓͘ḻ̵̨̡̳̜̥̄͒̽͒̃͌̏̂͒̈́̅́̓͝.̷̧̛͕̱̬̻̀̿̂̀̿͗́͌ ̵̢̛̹͕͈͖̳͚̟͚͌͆͒͑̔͊̃H̵̛͇͛͋̔̐̏̆̿̓̿̽̚͘͝͝ȇ̷̡̻̟̫͙̯̰̤͆ͅŗ̶̮̱͇̺̪̲̩͔̜̬̥̒̓̂͂͒̿͒̈́͋̕͜͠ ̷̦͙̮͈̮̎́̍̐̈́͗̉͗̀͐m̴̡̠̗͇̼͓̩̘̳̰͗̏ǒ̶̧͕͙̲̍͂ţ̵̮̦̻̺̹̝̯̮̲͔̤̘́̃̀̉̀̍͗̀͜h̵̻̺͓̜̞̞̤̹̣́̇̊̄̓̑͐̓̀̀͘͜͝ḛ̴͐͊̿̾͐͛̓̆͑̐̕r̴̡͙̖̹̿̾̾͑̎́̊͠ͅ ̶̥̺̑̑w̸̡̦̭̤̔̓̂̒͊͌́͑͘͘à̶̢̢̨̦̪̠̼̙̱͖̣͇̉́͆͆̒̀̒̎̅̽͂͒͊̚͜ͅṣ̷͗̎͌̎̿̏͊̿͠ ̵͙͙̜̣̜̠̯̖̭́̆̒̃̀̐̀̐͜f̴̧̡̞͚͕͚͖̫̰̮̺̪͍͂̾͜ͅį̷̡͔͔̰͎̳̼̽̓̈́͒͛̐́͂͝ģ̷͎̰͎̠̓́̚͜h̸̙͖̣͇̼͙̗̯͈͒̇̔̑͑̾́̊̈́̒͗ͅͅț̵̢͎͙͔̥̱̥̼̯̰͙̲̈́̎͛̃̅͆̀̎̌̈́̈̅̚̕͘͜ͅî̸̢̢̧̲̮̦̞͉̭̖̭̤̙̫̼͐͊̎̈́̾̓̽̑̎͝͠ñ̴̹̈́̊̉͠͠g̶̡̺͔̩̳͍̲̩̘͕͉̭̭͖̱̈́̍́̆͘ ̶̗̯̺̟̫̳̠̟͖̗̈́̽̆͋̎͋͑̒̆͑̄͂͘̚̚h̷̡̫̘̥̜͖̖̝̦̖̟͖̠́̂͆̚͜͜a̴̝̥͖̞̹͓̟̫̠͚̞̯̓͂͌͌̽̿̔͊ṟ̵̺̀̿̔̐̀́̌̓͋͊͘͝͝ͅd̸̢̢̛̺͍̠͖̥̰́̏͛̑͐́̇͘͝ͅ ̵͓̖̰̱̫̞͙͖̗̪̭̬͚̟́̏͌̓͗̉t̸͚̩̗̮̰̠͓̞͒̅̌͋̀͗͘͜͠͝ơ̴̥͖̰̙̋̔̈̔͊̐̈́̈́̅̉̓̕ ̸̨͉̦̹͋̌̔̃̀̂̔͊̆̈́̕͜c̷̢̨̩͉̑̋̊̓̅̀̄̊̓͝ḩ̵̮̖̻͕̯͛̎̍͂̌̀̈́̔͘̕a̸͙͑n̸͙̝̰͔̘͎̆̂͊̒̎͑͘͜g̴̻̥͚̬͚͚̲̱͔̼͖̙̰̈̓̑̈̏͠e̷̪̥̳͕͚͕̺̫̒̿͆ ̸̛̞̦͍̌͂̊̇̈̾t̷̨̠̞̻̩̰̆̽͛̎̏͗̌͑͂͗̎̏͘̕ẖ̶̛̹̳̪̇͗̒͊̂̔̂͠e̷͇͉̖͖̪̪̹̞̔͋͝ ̴͖͚̘͙̪̲͐̓̅̃̀͌̆̉̾́͘s̶̲͇̬̖͉̩̐̒̏̊̈́̾̿̄̌̕͝͝ţ̸͍̩̪̜̲̠̲̖̫̲̣̏͛̓̄̋̊͋̂̽͌̑͘͜͜͠a̴͚̟̠͉̭̗̪͑̓͛͗͗͛̈́̓̔͑͑͛̾͂t̶̳̻̼͕̗͎̬̻̺̩͔̬̥̝́̀͊͛͗̂͆̕̕e̶̪̱̭̺̱͓̰̭̼̺̯͂̈́͜ͅ ̴͇̫̱͍͖̮͔̼̄̋̊̈́̈́̕ͅt̵̛̻͍͈̼̼͒̍̿̂̌͑̈̊̓̇͗h̶̰̓̆̏̄͊̌̑͝ẹ̷̢̨̪̘̱̩̺̺̋̉y̴̫̭̮̤̮̬̭̼͊̍ ̵̧̡̞͓̖̯̬̰̫͕̭͖͛͐̉̓̋̐͗̇̋̂̐̀̂̈́ͅͅf̶̢̡̯͖͇̯̭̲̗̯̖̪̙̆̂̽́̓͑̋͘͜ơ̵̙̎̉͒͊́̅̾̽̕͘͠u̴̢̨̼͕̺̮̣̫̜͌̔́̈ͅͅn̶͇̾͝ḑ̵̡̟̩͂͝ ̷̡̨̘͖̹͇̋ņ̴̧̮͓̭͙̹̩͉̩̺͉̻̤͊̈́́̄̏͑͊̇͛̃ớ̴̦̜̙̖̦̎̈̇̐̓̒̉͆̒̂́̀̕ͅt̴̨͗̊̈͝ ̶̡̺̭̻͈͙͊̓̈̇̐͘͝ͅs̷̛͕͉͛̄̒͛͆̄̏̓̀͘̚i̶̩̣͕̬͉̬̼̗̞͎̬̳̠̺̿̋t̴̥̥̮͎̋̒̋͌̑͊ ̷͖̰̬͇̞̈̑̀̄̕͜͝ȁ̷̪̳͙͉͚̜͛̓̕͝r̵̡̻͖̉͐̈́̾ō̸͔̪͕̰͊́̓̌̈̐̎́̚͠ü̷̗͚̥̇͝͠n̷͎̝̯̯̟͑̌̾̆̊̎͆̕ḋ̸̮͓̰̬͔̠̭̤̱̩͐̔͋̉͛̾͝ ̷̲͇̲͍͆̓̈͂̉̐͛́͒͝͝͝ą̶̛̙̠̗̗̖̩͍̺͑̂̾̇̀̏́̈̄́̏ş̵̲̹̯͙̥̰̪͍̗͉̑̈́̅̓̉͊̾͝ ̶̛̘̯̈́͑̽͌́̉̿̍́̀͂̕͝ͅā̷̛̳͇͔̮̲̀͌̿̅̄̍͆͒ ̸̧̛͈̠̙̗̹̘̦͉̝̖̖̦̝̬̄͒p̸̬̣͔͈͉̝̻̣͂͋̉̂͂̕͜͝r̶̡̟͙̭̟̥̦͇͛͐̊̈́̓̆͒̚͝ͅi̵͙̭͖̯̲̳̻͔͊̄̑̓̐̆͗͒͂̚s̵͚̻̙͎͇̟̰̺̘̬̫̹̿͐̃̽̀̓͌̓̏̑̉̈͆o̷̻͇̠̤̓̋̄̉̏̀͘̚͝͝n̸̹͇̬̱̠͒̌̊ẹ̶̘̑̎r̷͙͎͖̻͔̦͛͌̕͠!̴̡̡̟̗̲̯̮̺̺̺͕̠̅̉͂̿͆̍́͐̓̂̎̎͘

Ḋ̵͚̙̍̉̆ų̸͔͚̟̼͕͍̰̭̺̙̞̓̔̉͜r̴̥̮͍̜͚̺̯͙̝̠̃̉̈́͛̈̃̈̈͗į̷̧̼͚͓͚̬̠̖̳̘̻̻̳̯̐̿̃̐͝n̷̡̞̣͗͗̒̏̏͌͜͝g̵̛̛̠̤̜̗̰̝̺̖̍͛̆̎̚ ̸̧̛̘̳̣͙͗͋̍͆̐͒̉͜ḧ̶̥̱͖́̌̽̂̃̊̔̑̈́̅͘è̸̫̺̖̔́̉̒̋̏̉r̵̢̢̠̗̰͕̳̓̌͑̊̂̀̀͜͝ ̴̗̬̱̺̍̃̽̊͋͐̂͆̓̈́̈́̇͆̾͘ş̶̢̨͇͇̣͖̩̦̖̺̲̿̈́͐̓̈̋͆̚͜ͅȩ̵̡̛̞̯̞̘͓̠͎̖͈͓̞̟͋͛̂̍́̽̌͌̂̾̐̚ͅa̷̢͖̥̗͎͊͒̀̾̀̊̋̀̉̔͆̌́͜ͅȑ̷̝̩̟̀͂͛̋̓̀̿͋̏́͂͜͠͠c̷̲̍̾̆̋̒̄̒̐h̴͈͕̬͎̿́̎̇̾̎̉̀̒̓ ̶̨̪̰͓̗̫̮̗͚̠̹̿̂̍̎͂͋̔̀̿̕͝͝ͅf̵̨̛̳̻̄͑͌̕͝ö̵̘͔̝̠͓̪̰̪̲͉͉̠̩́̅́͛͐͋̈́̊̋͐͆͜r̴̛͈̞͕̯̠͂̈́͒̅̀̆͠ ̵̢̡̖̙̺̘̟̳̇̍̓͆̆̀͋͑̂͂͑̕̚͠ä̵̢͍̖̤̦͖̗̘̹̩́́̌̎̇̿͂͑͗͑̍́ṅ̸̢̛̤͓͑̀̈́̊͌̀͊̽͘s̶̲͉̖͗͊̽̽̊̌̀̈́͛̇͠w̶̦̔͛́͌e̵̗̪̮͙͓̦̦̞͕͙̮̅̌̈̉͌́̏̏̔̂͠͠r̸̥̟̯͓͈̲̄̿̄̾̀̈́́̓̈́̕͘͠͝s̴̨̭̖͔̭̜̗̲̎̌̕̚͝ͅ ̷̗̘͔͇̻̹͉̺̖̲̞͍͚̿̋̇͊͆̀̓̏̍̔͛̈́͂t̸̢̐̎̿̀̒̅̀͜h̶̹͈̭̝̹̝͗̿͒ę̸̧̢͎̰͖̼̩͇͌͊̌̃̋̆ͅ ̶̛͙̝̓̌̊̓͑̾̑̏̍̄̋̂͗͝s̸̢̢̳̫̦̭̺̜͉̤̤͕̓̈́́̀̆͛ͅm̴̡̗̹͓̫̀̑̒̈́̀̄̀͗a̸̰͉̞̣̩̰̲̰͛̒̓̌l̶̗͎͈͍̱̈̊̿̔͐̋̿͋̒̈̕͠l̴̼͔̖̫͈̯̋̽̂̆̏̑̏̚͝ ̴̧̛̠̦͌̈́̈́̆S̷̢̛͍̮̥͉͒̾̉̐̐͆͊̎̋́͝p̶̰͕͓͕͚̖͉̳̅͜i̶̬̖̲̟͎͕̯͓̯͑͛̈́̅͜ŕ̵̢̗̥͚͙͖̥̰̳̦͌̂̍̕ỉ̸̢̨͍̹̣̳͎̞̪̻͔̜̯͊̄̎̑̓̌́̈́̒͘͘͘͜͠ţ̴̳͙̟̘̺͕͂́ͅu̶̲̟̾̽̊́̿̔̌̆̈́̇͐̆a̶̡̰͓͒̈͂l̵̢̝̲̜̙̱͎̻̞̒̋̿͂̍̉̃̀̐͂͋̽͌͝ ̵̡̟͇̼̝͇̬̯͙̹͇̩̱̣͒̿͌͑̔͋̐̆̆̃ͅV̶̱̹̤͉͛͌ȩ̸̡̧͇̺̲̲̤̯̔͐̃ͅͅş̷̛̭̻̜͇̖͈̟̯̹̹̽̔͌͗̆̈́͘s̸̠͔̘̤̩̦̭̗͍̒̋͑͘͠ę̸̯͍̻̺̙̲̗͇̑͂̏̋͛̎͌̕̚̕͝͠l̶̡̨̛̪̗̤͙̼̘͙̖̯͌̅̕ ̴̨͈̝̫̓̄̀̈́͂͑ľ̵̝̬̰̑į̸̻̈́͊̽b̵̥̳͖̙̅͠ř̸͚̺̗͈̻̬͎͎̯͉̟̥̝͘â̴̛̛̦̻̆̅̔̑r̵̪̒̃̇̀̃̆̀̉y̷̢̨̥͎̹͎͙͉͔̭̑,̵̥̖̪͖̗͎̞͍̹͓̝͈̍̉̊̂̒̓̕͜͝ ̸͈̀ą̷̛͎̬͚̭͎̟̻͎̯̫͖̹̪́n̵̪̩͖̝͛̉͆͗̀̃̐͆̋͑̊̑̈͝d̷̗͖̰̫̲̲̺̝͌̽͊̽̑͛̊͌͒̀̈́͐̾͒ͅ ̸̖̻̳͎̳̱͉̦̫̦̦͚̻͖̈́̈́͑̀ͅo̵̢̖͎̪̥͖͕̪̮̰͕̘̠͙̭͋͒̐̆̓̆f̷̡̗̙̹̮̹͔̲̟̀̍̚͜ ̷̧̛̼̩̼̺̮̫̳̱͆͒̏͠͠ţ̸̨̛̭̤̳͙̼̤͚͕͕̣̹͒̂̿͑̊͗̂͌̕͘͝h̶͎̲̣̺̥̹̓́̍̊̿̿̓͊̽̅́̚ę̷̧̟̮͚̯̪̪̱̃́̌̾̊i̸̛̥̮̣̍̈̓̿́͛̉̿́͘͝ŕ̷̨̫̳̤̫͎̻͚̻̰̠͖̠͒͗̿̍̓̈̀̈́͑̄̽̆́̐͜ͅ ̵̧̛̱̮̘̖͖͎̇̓͂̚͠t̷̢̞̟̟͖͍̣̃̌ͅĩ̵̢̪̝̞̹̱͙̔̓͘ͅm̴͕͖̯̪̜̪̉̈́̈̋͆ę̵̡͓̣̬̹̲̞͖̖̲̬̓͋̿́̽̋̾̌͂̏̊̚̕̕,̶̡̝̓̽̀ ̶̢̬͎̳͉̖͉͖̼̱̖͎̞̾́w̴̧͍͉͉͈̻̯̬̥̜͓̆́͗̾͒͗̔̔͊͝h̸̛̼̽̏̏͂̑̍̄̈̿̔̚͘̚͜i̸̘̹̲̓̑̓́̄̏̕͠c̶̛̭̞̼͈̝̫̤̙̤͋̒̋͊̔̀̊́͛̎̿̇̚h̴̢̬̱̮̱͓̲̥͎͈̺͐̂̕ ̷̡̨̧̤̦̱̘̦̗̺̦̹̟͍̘͐̐w̸͔̱̯̯̬̤̗̳͕̻̹̹̿̃̕̕͠ó̵͖̹̪̻̞̬̠̱͔̜̻̀̎̽̉̒̐̈́͋̈́u̸͎̗͖̪̲͗̀̀̏̑̄̽̈́́͑̉l̷̛̦̂̅̏̈́͋̐̒͑͛̓̐̕͠d̶̡̪̻̤͍̩̻̺͓̘͇̠̲͇͋͆̐͆̔͒̚ ̴̻̒̍̏̂́̈͝͝ḷ̷̤̂͒̋́̈́̇͊̀́͋͜͜͝͝ͅe̷͎̣̠̘̹̗͊̓̀͑͋̑̍̾̒͒̀̏̕͠ä̸̪̹͇̜͇̜͚͒͆̃͗͂̀̃̀̂̈́͠͠ͅḓ̸͎̮͔̮̖̞͖͕͉̖̙̇̂̅̈́̽̍̓̏͜͜ͅ ̶̧͉̟̀͋ȟ̴̢͔͖̹͖̱̰̺͚̝̳͖̣̞̰̽̃͒̿̑̉͊̆̊̀͗̕͝e̶͉̩͉̬͚̯̺̦͍͚͐͑͆͛̿̋̈́̆́̓̎̀͜͝r̷̖̪̀̆͗̏̑̈͆̈́̈́̓ ̷̲̲̱̦̖̿̄̎̕ẗ̷̢̗͎͉͈̯̱̰̹͖́̿̋͂̽͒̊̚͜͜ͅǫ̸̢̨̛̳͎̙͇̟̤̥̑̂̌̓̒͛̍̍̈́͗̇͊̚͠ ̸̥̮̖͖̼̈́́b̶̥̣͌͋̆́͂͝ě̴̡̜̜͔͚̿̉̇͋̕c̶̞͈͎̪͉͎̭̺͋̑̊̌̈́̄͝ọ̵̡̢̡̝͔͓̾ͅm̶̫̰̫̖͖̻̦͒͑̐̿̄͗͊̇̓͋̓̚ë̶͖́ ̶̡̦͚̣͎̬̼͍̱͂̇͛s̷̢̞̮̘̦͎͙̄̆̊͐̈͂́͌ͅt̴̨̤͚̝̤̯̣̥̬̗̞̥̟̂̊̓̔̊ͅͅr̸̥̣͔̞͚̃̍̈̎̃̀̿̃̕ơ̵̪̠͖̮̲̳̗͖̠͇̠̠̓̒͌̓͋̓̏́̍͗͂̇ͅn̸̡̨̟̙͓͇̗̙̈̒̇̌̄̽͒̋̾͊̒̎͘͜͠g̸̡͓̤̙̙̬͚̼͈͓͌̂̈͑̆̀̈́ ̸̱͒̍̿̀̄͗̈́̉̌̅̉̚͝͠͝e̷͔͒͊̀n̸̨̹͔̹̬͖̉̈̈́ò̷̡͓̥̲ų̴̣̠̬̥͍̫̈́̈́̓͒̄̓͝g̵̛̪̳͉̭͈̞̣̱͖͕̪̹͓̔͆̾̉̏͐͐̽̈͊̎̕͝h̴̛͚̥͗̂̀̋͐͐̊͌̓̍͠ ̴̺̥̦̭͉̺̜̓̿̀̓̈́̄͛̋̀̇͘̚͝͠ẗ̷̢̡͍̖̺͎̜̼̝̹̫̭̹̝̓o̵̥̼̣͇̝̫̍͌̀̄̄̽̍͗͋̃̈́ ̷̫̫͓̤̞̳͈̙̩̗̟̹̜̮̃̃̅̆̍̆̈͒̑̀͑̎̋̎f̵͓̜͍̥̜̘̥̙͔͉́̊̇̂̀͊̎͐ą̴͖̮͍̱̹̹̗͖̖͉̫̈̍̽̒͛̃̔̋c̶̭̹̙̤͊̾e̸͕̥̳͇̱̗̥̯̣͔͛́͆ ̶͙̱̗͔̲̟̥̳͌͛͆̍͑͒͂̇̀͛̔̕͝͝ḩ̸̢̣͎̤͐̈́͛ė̴̢̛͉̘̝͕̗̼͝ͅr̵̢̞̼̐̌͐͋͐͆̿̽͠ͅ ̸̤̜̳̊̉͆̀̆̄̈́̓̍̂̋̕̕͠m̸̫̥͉̻͓̯͚̗̠̯̣̆̂̓̀͐͌̓͐͌̐̈́̈̚ő̸̠̱̹̱͕͈͓̥̤͚̻̋̓t̵̼̬͉͖̐̓̀͝ḧ̶̨̠̮̻̭́̏̋̀̾͊͐̚ę̷̨̭̣̦̭̹̬̭̤͚͙̯̓͂͂͗̎r̵̲̬̫̭̮̹̲̻̼͈͊̊͆̀̈̾̓̂̓̈́̈́͆̍̕͝ ̵̤͎̝͔̤̇͒͒̀̀͜i̷̡̧̗̼͎̗̝͖̯̖͇̩̖͙͖͛̒̅̽̌́ñ̶̨̥̠̺̗̗̫̤͉̰̙̱̌͋͜͜͠ͅ ̴̢̯̙͙̥̯̲͉͙̱̳̓͆͒͐̊h̶̯̉̔́̆̐̈e̷̛͈̯̻͈̮̣̳̗̺̺͈͇̰̯̿̾̉͆͐̽̏̈́̌̅̍̿̂̚͜r̶͕͆̌̓̏͗̉͆̉͐̃͐̈́̈́̉͝ ̶̛̟͈̪̯̗͎̙̙̻͍̫̀͆̅̀̀̿͂̈́͊͋͆͊̒͆o̷̤̫̯̰̔w̶̛͉̓̾͋̾̈́̂͠n̶̢̛̪͔̥͍̞̖͔̤̦̥͉͓͔̆̂̈́̇̾͗̌̏͋̓ ̵͔̼͈̱͓͇͉͇͙͔̯̘͈̿̾̀̏̈́̋͋͠p̵̲͕̙̘͖͈͔̘͉̜̥̔͛̍ͅͅͅr̷̭̤̤̩̓è̴͍̗̘̖̲̬͇̩̰̗͖̤̑̔̀́̓̄̎́͐̕s̵̫̱͇̝̞̥̝̗̿̅͋͐̑́̄̆͆̀͌͜e̶̢̓́̀̊͆̊̌n̸̛̛̻̑̎̏̄͂̏̑̏̔̃͛̿͠t̶̘̯̩͌͌̑̂̊̊̐̏̏̂͒͠ͅ ̵̡̧͚͓̮͇̳̫̞̑̅̍̇̿̀̊̈́́̀̒̽̈́͒̍t̵̡̫̺̗̘̼͙̒̀͊̽̿͒̽̄͂̕̕͠ͅi̴͍̹̰̫͆͜͜͠ͅm̴̯̻̙̺͉̙͖̫͉̬̙̬͖̥̗͊̽̐̓̈̌̒̈́́e̶̺̟̖̺̲̙͙̞̻͍̮͌̿̾͒̾̓́͑̈́̓̓͋.̵̨̨̤͎̘̝̼̞͓̫̓͑̏͂̋ͅ
T̴̡̛̯͎͉̖͎̱̜̪͕̅̾͛̔̊͌́̿̇́̾͒͘ḫ̷̛̭̤͇̾̐̚͝͝e̴̢̞̬̖̳͉͕͍̮̬̊͜y̸̠͐̀ ̵̫̱̭̹̞̰̩͖̥͓̦̖̘͈̆̿̃͋̇̓r̸̡̙̱̖̠̟͈͉̀͑̎́̔̕ͅè̸̢̧̠̬̤͔͍̮̼͇̟͈̟̟͛̃̀̒̊͋̾̂̔̾́̐͜l̵̨̂̄͗͂̊͂́́̚͠ͅu̶̧̠͔̥̲̼̖͍͔̤̻̩͇̖͋͑̇͋̅̍̿̐̀̐̌̋̽͋̕c̵̖̐̈́͌t̴͎̺̮̯̦̰̮̱̳͕̲̖̘̘̤̍̀̍͋͝a̵̡̧̞̘̾̒͊̉̑́́̃͂̀͌͗͝n̶̢̥̣̼̣͎͇̺̩̭̬͍̖̣̓̽̊͆̓͌̈̆́̿̽̋͋̉ẗ̸̩̫̺̮͇̭͕̟́̉̈̍̄͌͝ĺ̶̢̢̧̘͇̰̬̞̝̭̫̻̈́̑̔̅̈́̆̕͠͠͝ͅỳ̶͖̳̬̺̱̲̺̣̫̮̹͍̱̹̆̀̓͠͝ ̶̪̈́͐̇͋̾͋͠͠͠a̷̧̢̹̫̤̯̯͇̦͊͜͠ḡ̶̮̭̝͉̤̩͈̰̙̟̤̖͛̃ͅṟ̶́͊̈́͆̏̉̅͛͐̈͗͘̚ę̶̥̠͖̼̺̹̲̘̯̈́̿ͅe̴̞͈̎̓͆̏̿̓̆̾̍́̾̍̎̂͝d̷̨̫̦͈͈̗͔̥̘͓͕̩̺̔́̔̈́̽̌̓̈́̈́̌̄̕͜͠ͅ,̶̯̖̘̼̰͓̤̰̺̜̮̔͌̆͗̑͠ͅ ̵̛̤͆̋̐̀̋͑̀͐̋̔͒͌̚w̸͉̭̬̖̩̫̏̀̂͒̅̈́͑̐̎̐́́́͆͝a̷͍̭̯̙̼̟̼̖̜̎̿͆̈̎̌̐́̀͘͝͠͠ṙ̵̛͚̺̲̺͙͙̈́̽͋̏̄̾̊̀̈͛ņ̷̗̰̰̰̭͓͙̘̘̹̈́̃͋̀͋͊͗̕͘ͅį̴̯͋͊͑̆͠ͅn̷̢̡̢̞͖͎̓͊̃̈́̎͗̑̍̈́̓̐͝͝͝ģ̵̙̙̥͙͇͉͙̐̿̓̿͛̄̀́͑͝ ̵̢͎̺̺͖͓̈̉̊́̿̾̈̆̊͂͝ͅḩ̷̡̬͕̥͓̹̬͉̟͆͜ͅe̵̱̣͌̈ŗ̸̛͈̩͈̭̩̼̖̖̎̆̏̓͂͝ ̶̨̡̫̟͖͎̥̟̲̥̲̹̠̻̤́͐̑͠t̷̨̟̜̣͇͒̌̀̎͋͆̋h̶̛̛̯͍͓̭̪̹͉͍̔̄̆͊̔̋͒̃̏͌̒̑a̴̢̡̖̪̭̰̳̼̺̜̩͙̋̄̅̏̓̓̿͗̓̑̈́̿͝͝͠t̷͉͓̯̬̘͖̖̭͎̝̗͍̩̒̀̋̈́̆̅̿̈̍͝͝ ̴̡̧̬̬̲̠̮͈̓̾͒̑̄́̎ͅo̵̡̡̥̖̱͓̪̣̣̬͑̉̄͐̉͒̂̀͋̾̏̽̾̒ň̷̡̛̟̩̘̮̭̯̹̱̥̙̜̙͔̬̀̒͘͠͝c̸͙̺͖̞͎̻̩̼̪̭̣̔͌ę̸͚͙̌͑̏̏͐̀̌̑̎ ̴̗͂͂̀͐̈́̈́̎̊s̶̩̼̺̟͌̀̈́̄̃̈́̊̊̅̏̈́͒͝͝h̸̡̨̧̲͍̠̻͇̦͎̦͙̤̩̀̓ͅȅ̷͓̝̹̣͇̗̬̙̎̉̉̈́͑̿͆̅͒̂͝͝ ̷̡̣̻͇̮̯̭̹̀̿t̶̮̟̗̘̞͍̎̐̕ŕ̸̨̦̠͍̹͛̇̋̈́̓̏̃̃̓̿͠ą̴̰̹̱̮͍̘̦̤͚̿͌͗͗̉̍ͅv̷̪̯̰̪͒̄̋̓͜ͅe̴̛̛̩̲̮͈̦̝̗̠͍͍̭̤̳͌̐́̈͂͂̓̉͆͆͒͜ͅl̵̛͇̳̜̞̘͔̺̾̿̾̓̈́̈́͛̋͐͐̎ệ̸͆̆͋d̴̩̫͈̟̀̒̓ ̷̡̣̤̺̣͕̝̲̇̓͌͒̋̕͜͝t̴̺̪̭͕̮̉̽̃̊̇͂͛́̐͂ͅh̶̢̳̙̹͈͕̯͈͑̽̍̾͒̄̑̄̅̏͝ŕ̴̻̥̈̎̅̽̿̾̽͒͋͠o̷͍̰̹̹̲̩̪̲̳̱̽͑̈́̔̇̈́̂͗͆̓̄̒̽͌͝u̷̡̧̼̮̫̰̫͇̫̳̱̹̺̿̀̑̀͐̓̓͠ͅͅg̷̭͉̞̃̋͂̄̉̐͗̀̈́̚̚h̴̛̛̪͆̅͌̔̈́͋̑͜͝ ̷̘̳̘̄s̸̻͖̹̬̣̟͉̩̠̮̥̙͈̲̳̒̂̀͗̅́h̶̖̟̬͔̤͆̐̈́̽͗͝ę̶͖̙̺̼̘͓͊͜ ̶̢̝͔̣̞̳͎̟̈́͊͒̀̾͋c̶̳̜̹͂́͒̈́̾̓͆̍̾̏͂͘ȍ̷̧͙̘̝͉̼̺̣̦̮̱͖͌̈̒u̷̘̙̜͉͗͑̄̿̃͌̈̑̈́͋͑̌l̸̛̝̩̰̙̣̬͂̀́̋̒͂͋̊̕͠ḍ̷̂̃̇̍͋̎͆̚͝ ̸̤̮̮͊̓n̴̦̪̐͑͊̅́̎̐̌̇͗o̷̡̱̬̰̪͕̰̲͓͖̤͐̿t̷̨̛͍̖̹͔̞̣̍̈͒̋̉̈̿͗̒̊̀͑͝͠ ̶̥̖͉̽̌̔͝ç̶̟͍͉̙͉̪̑̎̿̀̕͘͠o̸̝̞̣̱̙͉̯͓̓̀͆̐̀͂͘ͅm̴̫̮̻̜̹͈̘͒͂̂̆͒̾̓̒̇̃̍̕ę̶̛̤̖͕͚̲̼̞̉ͅ ̵͇̖͓̼̺͙͎̝̊̇͝͠b̵̧̜͚̜͓̤͙̲̹͇̭̳́̓̅̊̚̚͝ͅǎ̸̠̫͕̭ͅͅç̶̜̳̥̙͙̒̐͗̇̒̎͐̀̑̒̓̐̉͘k̸̛͔̉̾͆́͂̑̽̄̄͗̀͋͑͆.̸̡͇̭̝͎͕̝͋̓̒ ̶̮͉̯̖̘̼̼͂͌̋̈́̀̒̽Ạ̷̮̳̜̖͎̝͓͍̮̹͑̏̽̋̀̈́̿͜ļ̷̺̮̤̤̺̟̫͓̙͖̯̺̼͑̍̄͆̌̕̚͘̚ͅr̴̨̨̹͕͍̗̱̻̭̳̿͐̎͆̕͜͝ͅe̵͓̰͇̲͘a̸̡̡̛͔͙̞̼͕̝̬͍̓̈̌͊̈́̿̋̽̚͝͠ḑ̴̡͔̩̝̲͔̫̪̼̮̜̣̼̟̔̔̒̌̉̀y̵̗̳͍͇̙̞̮̠͑̄͌̆͂̆͐̂̿̌̆͝͠͠͠ ̷̧̠͔͓͇̘̌̒̌͊̒̏̽́͛̿̈̚w̴͔̥̭͕̓̎̽̈́̕h̸͇̖͎̗͓̬̼͇̪̥͍͍̭͛̔̐̾͋͛͜ȉ̵̧̨̡̨̛̯͇͔̤̗̬͙̠̜̼̇̃̈́̍́̈͑̓̏͆͠l̶̡̨̛̙̳͉̉͋̍̃̑͠ȩ̷̛͔͕̟͖̠͙͇͔̋̈́̅̊̾̍̀̓͑̾͘͜ ̶̨͎̞̯̻̩̗̦̗̠̻̞͍̩͋̏a̷̧̨̝̙͎̼͔͍̹̙͙͗̔̐̽͛̃ͅͅ ̴͙͒̄̄̈̀̂s̵̨̭̬̙͇̼̭͍̰̖̜̖͖̩̙̔͗̇̅̈́́̕͠ț̶̨̛̹̈́̑̑͑̀̌̋̉̐̿͒̽͜i̸̢̼̮̳̯̲̗̗̲͎͙̬̺͔̊͛͌͌͊͒́̎͘͝ḽ̸͖̖̠̠͕̯͈͕͛͋̈́̇̃ĺ̸̛̲̗̪̊̽̔̇̄̒̀͛̕ ̴̹̲̖̟̲͈͙̤̫̝̤͉͆̒̀͆̂̚b̴̛̫̝̬͔̤͛̃̾̉͌̋̑̋r̴̨̛̜̝̯͕̮̬̘̣̠̼͕͗̈́̍̈́́͗̋͋͛ḭ̵̛̼̣̪͕͓̗̖͎͚̺͐̃̀͜͠͝ǵ̶̛̠͔̖̬̹̜͈̟͉̖̖̖̬̐́̀̃̇̈́̊́̉͗̍̈́͜͠h̴̛͎͖̼̤̼̱̘͍̣̣̖̬̪͈̑̄̈̎͐̂͝ţ̵̬͚̘̟͗̈́̃̀̍ ̴̧̗̣̖͎̦̰͓͓̼̱̄͂͋̍͠g̸̺̳̈́͋̀̅̐̽̎̆͘͠͝͝͠ơ̷̡̤̜̙͈͓̞͈͕̮͇̙̤̿̑͋͊̒͗̑͂̀̉̅͘͝l̷͚̹̣̮̜͈̗͔̱̇̈́̃́̓̃͗́̌̌͌̀̔͘͜͜͜d̷̺̝͕̼̀̇̄̋̌́̈́ȇ̸̡̻̥͖̥̲̈̄̀̀̓̍̾̕̚̕͜͝ͅǹ̷͕̦̣̞̜̙̟̋́͜ ̵̨͔̪̫̺̭͓̣̰̯͇͚̔͒̾s̷̨̛͎̳͈̜̗̦͇̪̩͚̞͚̖̗̐̔̌͂̓̏͛̀̏̇͂̚̚ǘ̷̱̱̯̜̘̗̞̩̼͂ͅn̵͙̺͗͑̑̽͌̀̓̇͋͗́͘ ̶̫̲̜̝͒̍͋̄̀́̌͗̚͠s̷̘̟̓͂͋̏̀̂͒̓̈́̂͘̚͝͠ḩ̶̡̣̠͖̬͔͓̼̦̜͕̊̏͛͌͌̊̄̎̌̈́͘̚͝ö̸̩̜̰͙̰̔͑͂͗n̸̨̨̜̻̟̲͔͓͓̮͚̬͕͉͓̂̌͋̐̽́̓̈́̋̚e̶̖̼̥̰͘ ̸̺̯̜̤͈͛̈́̄͛́͌̂̉̑̃͘d̶̋̍̍͑͜͝ͅǫ̶̡̺̩̫͔̩̯͎̮̘̬̅̿̓̒̈́̽̍͜ͅw̶̡̧̧̡̩̹͈͓͙̪̣̻̥͙̪̃͐̐̈́̓̌̀́̀̿n̸̨̡̳̯͔̺͂̃̉͆̍̐̈̀̉ͅ ̶̭̈́͐͂̀͋̇̓́̕ò̷͇̝̒̄̋̓n̸͕͇͎̳̈̉̐̒̍̀͘͝ ̶̡̫̯̥̫̠͔̔̾͗͒̔̌͆͛͒̓͜͠h̸̢͚̣̄͗̀̑̽̒͘͘͠e̴͚̱̰̬̙̝̮͊̏͋̍̆͜ȓ̴̡̜͕͕̯̈́͂̽́̄̏̒̒ ̷̡̡̙̬̩͓̣̥̜̗̣̣̻̇͌̏͋͜͝š̸͖̩͎̾̈́͑͗̊̑̃ṁ̸̢͚͙͍͆ĭ̷̡͇̻͍̹͇͍̺̏͋͌͘͝͝l̵̯̿̀͒̕͘̚ȩ̸͈̟͎̲̦̖͇̖͖̗͎̗͖̈́̽͜.̶̨̛̠̤̺̪͉̠̜̲̲̽̌̀̑̐̋̈́̅͜͠ͅ

The hard part of her journey had only just begun.

Inventory

Messenger Bag
A leather rectangular bag with a large fold-over flap that buckles on the front to keep its contents stationary. Attached to a very long strap designed to be worn over one shoulder and across the upper body. This particular one is full of yellowing scrolls, parchment, a journal, and plenty of writing tools. It also carries the Crystal Knife in an external pouch.

Crystal Knife
A jagged foot-long knife crafted entirely out of a strange shimmering glass (iron durability). It can be used like a magnifying glass if looking through the smooth flat of the blade, and the hilt is wrapped in dark leather for a more sturdy grip.

Ancient Text
Collection of old fragile parchment wrapped in protective leather binding. An archaic book written in ancient Latin, hailing from the Great Roman Empire. Written by its current owner's favorite author, unsurprisingly a certain Philosopher who happens to be her personal hero.

Passive Abilities

Aging
The Vessel is still technically mortal, the only thing that stops her from dying is her body’s ability to grow and adapt, but inability to deteriorate from its prime. Once she reaches full maturity physically, the aging process will stop, and she will remain forever frozen to that age until death. Time is not a factor that can kill her (in the sense of dying naturally of old age), but that is the only form of “immortality” she possesses.

Mana Sensitivity
She is very sensitive to beings who are actively using mana within a 20 foot radius to herself. While she cannot sense specifics, the use of mana in an area can leave behind a detectable imprint allowing her to track much like a dog does with a scent. This is, of course, assuming the presence of mana is not being intentionally hidden by magics of any rank, and that the signature isn’t too old and faded.

Enhanced Perception
Her mind is able to process information--and reflexively act on said information--twice as fast as the average human. (x2 Mental Speed, x2 Processing Speed)

Photographic Memory
The Vessel’s capacity for storing information is even more impressive than the speed she collects and acts upon it. While the amount of space she has to keep all of this information is still within human capacity, she is capable of remembering things in very intricate detail as though her eyes are cameras and her mind a disk.

Semi-Intangibility
She does not have an entire ethereal form of her own, but she can temporarily change the makeup of her physical form to achieve semi-intangibility for extended periods of time. Achieving this form does unlock a few abilities, the most prominent being that she will be able to phase through any solid nonmagic base materials of up to iron in durability as though it does not exist, but only if said materials have a thickness of 20 feet maximum or less. In addition, when in this state she falls at a slowed gliding pace, allowing her to propel herself for greater distances, or fall greater distances without injuring herself (up to 20 feet for fall-gliding, 10 feet for jumping).
Should she be injured when in this state she bleeds mana, but any basic and minor nonmagic injuries and illnesses (colds, cuts, bruises, things a Paige healing spell could cure) she receives when in her normal solid form can be mended and cured by phasing into semi-intangibility. This state leaves her weaker to spiritual and magical attacks, but is incredibly resistant to base nonmagic attacks and materials.

Float!
Regardless of whether or not the Vessel is in her ghostly form, she can hover/float up to ten feet above the nearest solid surface (only accounting for surfaces that can hold her weight). While doing so she is only capable of moving at the same speed as she would if walking/running on the ground, and it still drains as much physical energy as doing either of those activities, even more if done for long periods of time.

Spiritualism: Paige

"Arguably one of the most powerful trees; Spiritualists possess the ability to speak to and beseech the spirits around themselves. This often requires much time, and also requires the spirits to agree with the mage's cause. One without conviction will not do well within this study. Spiritualists gain access to a unique mana type at Mage rank, which has been deemed "Spirit Force." Spirit Force has the capability to heal the soul, and at some level the flesh as well.​"

Paige Spells

Seeing-Eye Pack
After charging for two rotations--the first to summon a spirit, the second to begin the contract and the spell’s effects--Ava will gain an adorable ethereal friend which clings to her back and peeks out over her shoulder. Having no solid body allows the being to turn its head a full three-hundred-sixty degrees, which is important since its sight is why this spell is so useful! The spirit can see with eyes that have the same capacity for sight as the average human’s (within a 10 foot radius, scaling to 30 feet at Mage), except for the fact that its vision can bypass spells of its contractor’s rank (scaling up to Mage) or below specifically intended to hide from normal sight. Whatever it sees worthy of note can be whispered into Ava’s ear. This contract lasts for three rotations before a recast is required.

Speed Pact
This contract allows a spirit to sit atop the caster’s head, resting comfortably and unable to fall off (unless forcibly knocked/removed by spells of its rank or greater either energy based, designed to damage energy in some form, or designed to target spirits/the ethereal, scaling to Mage) in exchange for doubling their physical movement speed (x2 speed, stacking cap of x3). It takes two rotations of charging for this spell to take effect, the first being a summoning of the spirit, and the second creating the contract and allowing it to begin. After that the spell remains active for three rotations before a recast is required. Should removal of the spirit be successful it’s dismissed and a recast is required to bring the spell back up. Purely physical based attacks, even when dealing with magics, will pass through the spirit as though it doesn’t exist.

Bahh-Ram-Ewe
Ava can spend one rotation summoning an adorable fluffy ram spirit with nice tough horns. On the next she directs it toward a target up to 20 feet away and watches it take off, intending to smack into their center of mass with those aforementioned horns (equal in durability to the spell’s rank, scaling to Mage). It behaves like a construct when contested (again, equal in durability to the spell’s rank, scaling to Mage) but only hits with about as much force as a base human punch, and runs as fast as the average base human can sprint. Once the attack has been carried out, regardless of whether it succeeds or fails, the contract is finished and a recast is required.
